util_bar(mw.utilization);\n                println!(\"    {:10} {:5.1}%  {}\", mw.model, mw.utilization, bar);\n            }\n        }\n\n        if acct.burn_rate_per_min > 0.0 {\n            println!(\"  Burn rate:  {:.0} tokens/min\", acct.burn_rate_per_min);\n            if let Some(mins) = acct.forecast_full_5h_min {\n                if mins > 0.0 {\n                    println!(\"  Forecast:   5h full in {}\", format_minutes(mins));\n                } else {\n                    println!(\"  Forecast:   5h window full\");\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        println!(\n            \"  Turns:      {} (5h)  {} (7d)\",\n            acct.turns_5h, acct.turns_7d\n        );\n        println!();\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\nfn util_bar(util: f64) -> String {\n    let filled = ((util / 100.0) * 20.0).round() as usize;\n    let filled = filled.min(20);\n    let empty = 20 - filled;\n    format!(\"[{}{}]\", \"█\".repeat(filled), \"░\".repeat(empty))\n}\n\nfn format_resets_at(dt: chrono::DateTime<chrono::Utc>) -> String {\n    use chrono::Utc;\n    let now = Utc::now();\n    let delta = dt - now;\n    let total_secs = delta.num_seconds();\n    if total_secs <= 0 {\n        return \"now\".to_string();\n    }\n    let hours = total_secs / 3600;\n    let mins = (total_secs % 3600) / 60;\n    if hours > 0 {\n        format!(\"in {}h {}m\", hours, mins)\n    } else {\n        format!(\"in {}m\", mins)\n    }\n}\n\nfn format_minutes(mins: f64) -> String {\n    if mins < 60.0 {\n        format!(\"{:.0}m\", mins)\n    } else {\n        format!(\"{:.1}h\", mins / 60.0)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Run transcribe command\nfn run_transcribe(input: PathBuf, wait: bool, timeout: u64, json: bool) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config()?;\n\n    if !config.whisper.enabled {\n        eprintln!(\n            \"Whisper transcription is disabled.\\n\\\n             Enable it in config.toml:\\n\\n\\\n             [whisper]\\n\\\n             enabled = true\\n\\\n             model_path = \\\"~/.agentscribe/models/ggml-base.bin\\\"\\n\\\n             backend = \\\"whisper_cpp\\\"\"\n        );\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    if !input.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"File not found: {}\", input.display());\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    let rt = tokio::runtime::Runtime::new().map_err(|e| {\n        crate::error::AgentScribeError::Transcription(format!(\n            \"failed to create async runtime: {}\",\n            e\n        ))\n    })?;\n\n    // For fire-and-forget (--no-wait), submit to the queue and print job ID.\n    if !wait {\n        let job_id = rt.block_on(async {\n            let queue = crate::transcription::TranscriptionQueue::new(\n                config.whisper.clone(),\n                config.redaction.clone(),\n            );\n            queue.submit(input, config.whisper.max_retries).await\n        })?;\n        println!(\"Transcription job submitted: {}\", job_id);\n        return Ok(());\n    }\n\n    // Synchronous path: run transcription and wait for the result.\n    let job = rt.block_on(async {\n        let queue = crate::transcription::TranscriptionQueue::new(\n            config.whisper.clone(),\n            config.redaction.clone(),\n        );\n        let job_id = queue.submit(input, config.whisper.max_retries).await?;\n        queue\n            .wait_for_job(&job_id, std::time::Duration::from_secs(timeout))\n            .await\n    })?;\n\n    let result = match job.result {\n        Some(r) => r,\n        None => {\n            eprintln!(\n                \"Transcription failed: {}\",\n                job.error.as_deref().unwrap_or(\"unknown error\")\n            );\n            std::process::exit(1);\n        }\n    };\n\n    // ── Output ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n    if json {\n        println!(\n            \"{}\",\n            serde_json::to_string_pretty(&result).map_err(|e| {\n                crate::error::AgentScribeError::Transcription(format!(\n                    \"JSON serialization failed: {}\",\n                    e\n                ))\n            })?\n        );\n    } else {\n        // Warning card for degraded results.\n        if result.has_warnings {\n            eprintln!(\"┌─ TRANSCRIPTION WARNINGS ─────────────────────────────────────┐\");\n            for w in &result.warnings {\n                eprintln!(\"│  {}\", w);\n            }\n            eprintln!(\"└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\");\n        }\n\n        println!(\"{}\", result.full_text);\n\n        // Summary line with timestamp granularity info.\n        let level = match result.timestamp_level {\n            crate::transcription::TimestampLevel::Word => \"word-level\",\n            crate::transcription::TimestampLevel::Utterance => \"utterance-level (fallback)\",\n        };\n        eprintln!(\n            \"[{} segments, {}, transcribed at {}]\",\n            result.segment_count(),\n            level,\n            result.transcribed_at.to_rfc3339(),\n        );\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Run digest command\nfn run_digest(since: String, output: Option<String>, json: bool) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config()?;\n    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n\n    if !data_dir.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"AgentScribe not initialized. Run 'agentscribe config init' to set up.\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    let since_dt = search::parse_datetime(&since)?;\n\n    let opts = crate::digest::DigestOptions {\n        since: since_dt,\n        output: output.clone(),\n        json,\n    };\n\n    let digest_output = crate::digest::generate_digest(&data_dir, &opts, &config)?;\n\n    let content = if json {\n        crate::digest::format_json(&digest_output)\n    } else {\n        crate::digest::format_markdown(&digest_output)\n    };\n\n    if let Some(path) = output {\n        std::fs::write(&path, &content)?;\n        eprintln!(\"Digest written to {}\", path);\n    } else {\n        print!(\"{}\", content);\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Run context command: pre-task priming query for agent workers\nfn run_context(\n    query: String,\n    token_budget: usize,\n    project: Option<PathBuf>,\n    json: bool,\n) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config()?;\n    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n\n    if !data_dir.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"AgentScribe not initialized. Run 'agentscribe config init' to set up.\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    // Store the current_dir in a variable to avoid lifetime issues\n    let current_dir = std::env::current_dir().ok();\n    let project_path = if let Some(ref p) = project {\n        Some(p.as_path())\n    } else {\n        current_dir.as_deref()\n    };\n\n    let pack = crate::search::context_pack(&data_dir, &query, token_budget, project_path)?;\n\n    if json {\n        println!(\"{}\", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&pack).unwrap());\n    } else {\n        print!(\"{}\", pack.format_text());\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Run render command: export a session as HTML or Markdown\nfn run_render(session_id: String, output: Option<PathBuf>, format: String) -> Result<()> {\n    let config = load_config()?;\n    let data_dir = config.data_dir()?;\n\n    if !data_dir.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"AgentScribe not initialized. Run 'agentscribe config init' to set up.\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    let sessions_dir = data_dir.join(\"sessions\");\n    if !sessions_dir.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\"No sessions directory found. Run 'agentscribe scrape' first.\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    // Parse session ID to get agent and session parts\n    let parts: Vec<&str> = session_id.splitn(2, '/').collect();\n    if parts.len() != 2 {\n        eprintln!(\"Invalid session ID format. Expected: <agent>/<session-id>\");\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    let session_path = sessions_dir\n        .join(parts[0])\n        .join(format!(\"{}.jsonl\", parts[1]));\n\n    if !session_path.exists() {\n        eprintln!(\n            \"Session '{}' not found at {}\",\n            session_id,\n            session_path.display()\n        );\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    // Read session events\n    let events = read_session_events(&sessions_dir, &session_id)?;\n    if events.is_empty() {\n        eprintln!(\"Session '{}' has no events\", session_id);\n        std::process::exit(1);\n    }\n\n    // Build manifest from events\n    let manifest = crate::index::build_manifest_from_events(\n        &events,\n        &session_id,\n        parts[0],\n        events.first().and_then(|e| e.project.as_deref()),\n        events.first().and_then(|e| e.model.as_deref()),\n    );\n\n    // Render based on format\n    let content = match format.as_str() {\n        \"markdown\" | \"md\" => crate::render::render_markdown(&events, &manifest)?,\n        \"html\" => crate::render::render_html(&events, &manifest)?,\n        _ => {\n            eprintln!(\"Unknown format '{}'. Use 'html' or 'markdown'.\", format);\n            std::process::exit(1);\n        }\n    };\n\n    // Output to file or stdout\n    if let Some(path) = output {\n        std::fs::write(&path, &content)?;\n        eprintln!(\"Rendered session '{}' to {}\", session_id, path.display());\n    } else {\n        print!(\"{}\", content);\n    }\n\n    Ok(())\n}\n","numLines":2761,"startLine":1,"totalLines":2761}}}

The JSON output includes the `source_agent` field for filtering in downstream tools.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Finding and Fixing Recurring Errors\n\nYou keep hitting the same errors across different projects. Overridden by `AGENTSCRIBE_DATA_DIR` env var. |\n14\t| `--config <path>` | `-c` | `~/.agentscribe/config.toml` | Path to global config file. |\n15\t| `--json` | `-j` | off | Output in JSON format. Applies to all commands. When enabled, all output is machine-readable JSON — no human-formatted tables or progress bars. |\n16\t| `--quiet` | `-q` | off | Suppress non-essential output. Errors still print to stderr. |\n17\t| `--verbose` | `-v` | off | Enable debug-level logging to stderr. Repeatable (`-vv` for trace). |\n18\t| `--color <when>` | | `auto` | Color output: `auto`, `always`, `never`. Auto-detects terminal. |\n19\t| `--help` | `-h` | | Show help for the current command. |\n20\t| `--version` | `-V` | | Print version and exit. |\n21\t\n22\t---\n23\t\n24\t## `agentscribe scrape`\n25\t\n26\tDiscover agent log files, parse them, normalize to canonical format, and write to the sessions directory. Updates the Tantivy index incrementally.\n27\t\n28\t### Usage\n29\t\n30\t```\n31\tagentscribe scrape [options]\n32\t```\n33\t\n34\t### Options\n35\t\n36\t| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n37\t|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n38\t| `--plugin <name>` | `-p` | all plugins | Scrape only the named plugin. Can be repeated (`-p claude-code -p aider`). |\n39\t| `--project <path>` | | all projects | Scrape only sessions from the given project directory. Matches against the session's `project` field. |\n40\t| `--file <path>` | | | Scrape a single source file. Useful for testing a plugin against one log file. Requires `--plugin`. |\n41\t| `--dry-run` | `-n` | off | Show what would be scraped without writing any files or updating the index. |\n42\t| `--output-events` | | off | With `--dry-run`, print each parsed event as a JSON object to stdout. Use to verify field mapping. |\n43\t| `--force` | `-f` | off | Ignore scrape state (last-seen offsets) and re-scrape everything. Does not delete existing sessions — deduplicates by session ID. |\n44\t| `--no-index` | | off | Write session files but skip Tantivy index update. Useful for bulk imports where you'll `index rebuild` afterward. |\n45\t| `--since <datetime>` | | | Only scrape sessions with activity after this timestamp. ISO 8601 or relative (`24h`, `7d`, `1w`). |\n46\t\n47\t### Examples\n48\t\n49\t```bash\n50\t# Scrape all configured plugins\n51\tagentscribe scrape\n52\t\n53\t# Scrape only Claude Code sessions\n54\tagentscribe scrape --plugin claude-code\n55\t\n56\t# Dry-run with event output to verify a new plugin\n57\tagentscribe scrape --plugin pilot --dry-run --output-events\n58\t\n59\t# Scrape a single file for debugging\n60\tagentscribe scrape --plugin aider --file ~/myproject/.aider.chat.history.md\n61\t\n62\t# Re-scrape everything from scratch\n63\tagentscribe scrape --force\n64\t\n65\t# Bulk import without indexing (rebuild index after)\n66\tagentscribe scrape --force --no-index\n67\tagentscribe index rebuild\n68\t```\n69\t\n70\t### Output\n71\t\n72\tHuman-readable (default):\n73\t```\n74\tScraping claude-code...\n75\t  Found 12 new sessions (skipped 89 unchanged)\n76\t  Wrote 12 session files to ~/.agentscribe/sessions/claude-code/\n77\tScraping aider...\n78\t  Found 3 new sessions (skipped 5 unchanged)\n79\t  Wrote 3 session files to ~/.agentscribe/sessions/aider/\n80\tIndex updated: 15 documents added (1,262 total)\n81\t```\n82\t\n83\tJSON (`--json`):\n84\t```json\n85\t{\n86\t  \"plugins\": [\n87\t    {\n88\t      \"name\": \"claude-code\",\n89\t      \"new_sessions\": 12,\n90\t      \"skipped_sessions\": 89,\n91\t      \"errors\": []\n92\t    },\n93\t    {\n94\t      \"name\": \"aider\",\n95\t      \"new_sessions\": 3,\n96\t      \"skipped_sessions\": 5,\n97\t      \"errors\": []\n98\t    }\n99\t  ],\n100\t  \"index\": {\n101\t    \"documents_added\": 15,\n102\t    \"total_documents\": 1262\n103\t  }\n104\t}\n105\t```\n106\t\n107\t### Exit Codes\n108\t\n109\t| Code | Meaning |\n110\t|------|---------|\n111\t| 0 | Success — all plugins scraped without errors |\n112\t| 1 | Partial failure — some plugins had errors, others succeeded. Check `errors` in JSON output. |\n113\t| 2 | Total failure — no sessions scraped. Likely a config or permissions issue. |\n114\t\n115\t---\n116\t\n117\t## `agentscribe search`\n118\t\n119\tQuery the Tantivy index for matching sessions. The primary interface for agents seeking past solutions.\n120\t\n121\t### Usage\n122\t\n123\t```\n124\tagentscribe search <query> [options]\n125\t```\n126\t\n127\t### Arguments\n128\t\n129\t| Argument | Required | Description |\n130\t|----------|----------|-------------|\n131\t| `<query>` | no* | Search query string. Supports Tantivy query syntax: `+required -excluded \"exact phrase\"`, field-scoped queries (`content:migration`), boolean operators (`AND`, `OR`, `NOT`), fuzzy terms (`migrat~1`), wildcard (`migrat*`). Required unless using `--error`, `--code`, `--solution-only`, `--like`, or `--session`. |\n132\t\n133\t### Options\n134\t\n135\t| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n136\t|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n137\t| `--error <pattern>` | | | Search error fingerprints. Matches against normalized error patterns (e.g., `ConnectionError:Connection refused`). |\n138\t| `--code <query>` | | | Search extracted code artifacts by content. |\n139\t| `--lang <language>` | | | Language filter for `--code` search (e.g., `rust`, `python`, `typescript`). |\n140\t| `--solution-only` | | off | Return only sessions that have an extracted solution. |\n141\t| `--like <session-id>` | | | Find sessions similar to the given session ID using TF-IDF similarity. |\n142\t| `--session <id>` | | | Retrieve a specific session by ID. Ignores query and filters. Returns the full session content. |\n143\t| `--max-results <n>` | `-n` | `10` | Maximum number of sessions to return. |\n144\t| `--snippet-length <n>` | | `200` | Maximum character length of content snippets per result. Set to `0` to omit snippets. |\n145\t| `--token-budget <n>` | | | Token budget for greedy knapsack context packing. Optimally packs results within the token limit. |\n146\t| `--agent <name>` | `-a` | all | Filter to sessions from this agent type. Can be repeated. |\n147\t| `--project <path>` | | all | Filter to sessions from this project directory. |\n148\t| `--since <datetime>` | | | Only match sessions after this timestamp. ISO 8601 or relative (`24h`, `7d`, `1w`). |\n149\t| `--before <datetime>` | | | Only match sessions before this timestamp. |\n150\t| `--tag <tag>` | `-t` | | Filter by tag. Can be repeated (AND logic). |\n151\t| `--outcome <outcome>` | | | Filter by session outcome: `success`, `failure`, `abandoned`, `unknown`. |\n152\t| `--type <type>` | | all | Filter by document type: `session`, `code_artifact`. |\n153\t| `--model <name>` | | all | Filter by LLM model name. |\n154\t| `--sort <field>` | `-s` | `relevance` | Sort order: `relevance` (BM25 score), `newest`, `oldest`, `turns`. |\n155\t| `--offset <n>` | | `0` | Skip first N results. For pagination. |\n156\t| `--fuzzy` | | off | Enable fuzzy matching on all query terms (Levenshtein distance 1). Useful when agents don't know exact terminology. |\n157\t\n158\t### Examples\n159\t\n160\t```bash\n161\t# Basic search\n162\tagentscribe search \"postgres migration\"\n163\t\n164\t# Agent-oriented: JSON output, limited results, short snippets\n165\tagentscribe search \"database connection timeout\" --json -n 3 --snippet-length 150\n166\t\n167\t# Scoped to a specific agent and project\n168\tagentscribe search \"deploy\" --agent claude-code --project /home/coding/myapp\n169\t\n170\t# Recent sessions only\n171\tagentscribe search \"build failure\" --since 7d\n172\t\n173\t# Fuzzy search for misspellings or approximate terms\n174\tagentscribe search \"kuberntes\" --fuzzy\n175\t\n176\t# Exact phrase search\n177\tagentscribe search '\"connection pool exhausted\"'\n178\t\n179\t# Advanced Tantivy query syntax\n180\tagentscribe search '+content:migration +agent:claude-code -content:rollback'\n181\t\n182\t# Retrieve a specific session's full content\n183\tagentscribe search --session claude-code/83f5a4e7\n184\t\n185\t# Search by error fingerprint\n186\tagentscribe search --error \"ConnectionError\"\n187\t\n188\t# Search code artifacts\n189\tagentscribe search --code \"fn migrate\" --lang rust\n190\t\n191\t# Find sessions with extracted solutions\n192\tagentscribe search \"auth token\" --solution-only\n193\t\n194\t# Find similar sessions\n195\tagentscribe search --like claude-code/83f5a4e7\n196\t\n197\t# Context packing for agent prompts (fit within token budget)\n198\tagentscribe search \"error handling\" --token-budget 4000 --json\n199\t\n200\t# Filter by document type and model\n201\tagentscribe search \"refactor\" --type code_artifact --model claude-sonnet-4-20250514\n202\t```\n203\t\n204\t### Output\n205\t\n206\tHuman-readable (default):\n207\t```\n208\t3 results for \"postgres migration\" (searched 1,262 sessions in 4ms)\n209\t\n210\t[1] claude-code/83f5a4e7  (score: 8.42)\n211\t    Project:  /home/coding/myapp\n212\t    Date:     2026-03-14 10:30\n213\t    Turns:    42\n214\t    Outcome:  success\n215\t    Summary:  Migrated Postgres schema from v3 to v4, added rollback script\n216\t    Snippet:  ...ran ALTER TABLE to add the new columns, then backfilled\n217\t              existing rows. The migration took 3 minutes on a 2M row table...\n218\t\n219\t[2] aider/session-2026-03-10  (score: 6.18)\n220\t    Project:  /home/coding/api-server\n221\t    Date:     2026-03-10 14:15\n222\t    Turns:    18\n223\t    Outcome:  success\n224\t    Summary:  Fixed Postgres connection pooling, added retry logic\n225\t    Snippet:  ...the connection pool was exhausting under load because\n226\t              max_connections was set to 10. Bumped to 50 and added...\n227\t\n228\t[3] codex/abc-thread-123  (score: 4.01)\n229\t    Project:  /home/coding/data-pipeline\n230\t    Date:     2026-03-08 09:00\n231\t    Turns:    7\n232\t    Outcome:  failure\n233\t    Summary:  Attempted Postgres 14->16 upgrade, hit extension incompatibility\n234\t    Snippet:  ...pg_trgm extension not available in pg16 container image.\n235\t              Rolled back to pg14 and opened an issue...\n236\t```\n237\t\n238\tJSON (`--json`):\n239\t```json\n240\t{\n241\t  \"query\": \"postgres migration\",\n242\t  \"total_matches\": 3,\n243\t  \"search_time_ms\": 4,\n244\t  \"sessions_searched\": 1262,\n245\t  \"results\": [\n246\t    {\n247\t      \"session_id\": \"claude-code/83f5a4e7\",\n248\t      \"source_agent\": \"claude-code\",\n249\t      \"project\": \"/home/coding/myapp\",\n250\t      \"timestamp\": \"2026-03-14T10:30:00Z\",\n251\t      \"turns\": 42,\n252\t      \"outcome\": \"success\",\n253\t      \"score\": 8.42,\n254\t      \"summary\": \"Migrated Postgres schema from v3 to v4, added rollback script\",\n255\t      \"snippet\": \"...ran ALTER TABLE to add the new columns, then backfilled existing rows. The migration took 3 minutes on a 2M row table...\",\n256\t      \"tags\": [\"postgres\", \"migration\", \"schema\", \"alter-table\"]\n257\t    }\n258\t  ]\n259\t}\n260\t```\n261\t\n262\t### Full Session Retrieval\n263\t\n264\tWhen `--session <id>` is used, returns the complete normalized conversation:\n265\t\n266\t```bash\n267\tagentscribe search --session claude-code/83f5a4e7 --json\n268\t```\n269\t\n270\t```json\n271\t{\n272\t  \"session_id\": \"claude-code/83f5a4e7\",\n273\t  \"source_agent\": \"claude-code\",\n274\t  \"project\": \"/home/coding/myapp\",\n275\t  \"started\": \"2026-03-14T10:30:00Z\",\n276\t  \"ended\": \"2026-03-14T11:15:00Z\",\n277\t  \"turns\": 42,\n278\t  \"outcome\": \"success\",\n279\t  \"summary\": \"Migrated Postgres schema from v3 to v4, added rollback script\",\n280\t  \"events\": [\n281\t    {\n282\t      \"ts\": \"2026-03-14T10:30:00Z\",\n283\t      \"role\": \"user\",\n284\t      \"content\": \"I need to migrate the Postgres schema from v3 to v4...\"\n285\t    },\n286\t    {\n287\t      \"ts\": \"2026-03-14T10:30:15Z\",\n288\t      \"role\": \"assistant\",\n289\t      \"content\": \"I'll create a migration script that...\"\n290\t    }\n291\t  ]\n292\t}\n293\t```\n294\t\n295\t### Exit Codes\n296\t\n297\t| Code | Meaning |\n298\t|------|---------|\n299\t| 0 | Results found |\n300\t| 0 | No results (empty results array, not an error) |\n301\t| 1 | Query parse error or invalid filter |\n302\t| 2 | Index not found — run `agentscribe scrape` first |\n303\t\n304\t---\n305\t\n306\t## `agentscribe index`\n307\t\n308\tManage the Tantivy search index.\n309\t\n310\t### Usage\n311\t\n312\t```\n313\tagentscribe index <subcommand> [options]\n314\t```\n315\t\n316\t### Subcommands\n317\t\n318\t#### `agentscribe index rebuild`\n319\t\n320\tDrop the existing Tantivy index and rebuild it from all normalized session files. Use after a bulk import, after changing the schema, or to recover from index corruption.\n321\t\n322\t| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n323\t|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n324\t| `--plugin <name>` | `-p` | all | Only re-index sessions from this plugin. |\n325\t| `--heap-size <mb>` | | `50` | Tantivy writer heap size in MB. Higher = faster indexing, more RAM. |\n326\t\n327\t```bash\n328\t# Full rebuild\n329\tagentscribe index rebuild\n330\t\n331\t# Rebuild only Claude Code sessions\n332\tagentscribe index rebuild --plugin claude-code\n333\t\n334\t# Fast rebuild with more memory\n335\tagentscribe index rebuild --heap-size 100\n336\t```\n337\t\n338\tOutput:\n339\t```\n340\tDropping existing index...\n341\tRebuilding from 1,262 session files...\n342\t  [========================================] 1262/1262 (47/s)\n343\tIndex rebuilt in 26.8s\n344\t```\n345\t\n346\t#### `agentscribe index stats`\n347\t\n348\tShow index statistics.\n349\t\n350\t```bash\n351\tagentscribe index stats\n352\t```\n353\t\n354\tOutput:\n355\t```\n356\tTantivy index at ~/.agentscribe/index/tantivy/\n357\t  Documents:    1,262\n358\t  Segments:     4\n359\t  Size on disk: 38 MB\n360\t  Last updated: 2026-03-16 12:30:00\n361\t  Fields:       content, summary, session_id, source_agent, project, tags, timestamp, turn_count, outcome\n362\t```\n363\t\n364\tJSON (`--json`):\n365\t```json\n366\t{\n367\t  \"path\": \"~/.agentscribe/index/tantivy/\",\n368\t  \"documents\": 1262,\n369\t  \"segments\": 4,\n370\t  \"size_bytes\": 39845888,\n371\t  \"last_updated\": \"2026-03-16T12:30:00Z\",\n372\t  \"fields\": [\"content\", \"summary\", \"session_id\", \"source_agent\", \"project\", \"tags\", \"timestamp\", \"turn_count\", \"outcome\"]\n373\t}\n374\t```\n375\t\n376\t#### `agentscribe index optimize`\n377\t\n378\tForce-merge Tantivy segments for better query performance. Normally unnecessary — Tantivy auto-merges in the background.\n379\t\n380\t```bash\n381\tagentscribe index optimize\n382\t```\n383\t\n384\tOutput:\n385\t```\n386\tMerging 4 segments into 1... done (3.2s)\n387\tIndex size: 38 MB -> 35 MB\n388\t```\n389\t\n390\t### Exit Codes\n391\t\n392\t| Code | Meaning |\n393\t|------|---------|\n394\t| 0 | Success |\n395\t| 1 | Index error (corruption, missing session files) |\n396\t| 2 | No session files found — run `agentscribe scrape` first |\n397\t\n398\t---\n399\t\n400\t## `agentscribe status`\n401\t\n402\tShow a summary of what AgentScribe knows: tracked agents, session counts, last scrape time, daemon state, and disk usage.\n403\t\n404\t### Usage\n405\t\n406\t```\n407\tagentscribe status [options]\n408\t```\n409\t\n410\t### Options\n411\t\n412\t| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n413\t|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n414\t| `--plugin <name>` | `-p` | all | Show status for a specific plugin only. |\n415\t\n416\t### Examples\n417\t\n418\t```bash\n419\tagentscribe status\n420\t```\n421\t\n422\tOutput:\n423\t```\n424\tAgentScribe v0.1.0\n425\tData dir: ~/.agentscribe (142 MB)\n426\t\n427\tDaemon: running (PID 12345, uptime 3d 14h, RSS 12 MB)\n428\t\n429\tPlugins:\n430\t  claude-code    89 sessions   last scraped 2m ago     ~/.claude/projects/*/*.jsonl\n431\t  aider           8 sessions   last scraped 2m ago     ~/projects/*/.aider.chat.history.md\n432\t  codex          14 sessions   last scraped 2m ago     ~/.codex/sessions/**/*.jsonl\n433\t  opencode        0 sessions   never scraped           ~/.local/share/opencode/storage/\n434\t\n435\tIndex: 111 documents, 4 segments, 38 MB on disk\n436\t\n437\tScrape state: incremental (tracking offsets for 6 source paths)\n438\t```\n439\t\n440\tJSON (`--json`):\n441\t```json\n442\t{\n443\t  \"version\": \"0.1.0\",\n444\t  \"data_dir\": \"~/.agentscribe\",\n445\t  \"data_dir_bytes\": 148897792,\n446\t  \"daemon\": {\n447\t    \"running\": true,\n448\t    \"pid\": 12345,\n449\t    \"uptime_seconds\": 309600,\n450\t    \"rss_bytes\": 12582912\n451\t  },\n452\t  \"plugins\": [\n453\t    {\n454\t      \"name\": \"claude-code\",\n455\t      \"sessions\": 89,\n456\t      \"last_scraped\": \"2026-03-16T12:28:00Z\",\n457\t      \"source_paths\": [\"~/.claude/projects/*/*.jsonl\"]\n458\t    }\n459\t  ],\n460\t  \"index\": {\n461\t    \"documents\": 111,\n462\t    \"segments\": 4,\n463\t    \"size_bytes\": 39845888\n464\t  }\n465\t}\n466\t```\n467\t\n468\t### Exit Codes\n469\t\n470\t| Code | Meaning |\n471\t|------|---------|\n472\t| 0 | Success |\n473\t| 1 | Data dir not found or not initialized |\n474\t\n475\t---\n476\t\n477\t## `agentscribe daemon`\n478\t\n479\tManage the background daemon that watches for new log data and scrapes automatically.\n480\t\n481\t### Usage\n482\t\n483\t```\n484\tagentscribe daemon <subcommand> [options]\n485\t```\n486\t\n487\t### Subcommands\n488\t\n489\t#### `agentscribe daemon start`\n490\t\n491\tStart the daemon in the background. Writes PID to `~/.agentscribe/agentscribe.pid`. Logs to `~/.agentscribe/daemon.log`.\n492\t\n493\t| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n494\t|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n495\t| `--mcp` | | off | Enable MCP server on the daemon. Listens on a Unix socket at `~/.agentscribe/mcp.sock`. |\n496\t| `--log-level <level>` | | `info` | Daemon log level: `error`, `warn`, `info`, `debug`, `trace`. |\n497\t| `--scrape-debounce <duration>` | | `5s` | Wait this long after a file change before scraping. Prevents thrashing during active agent sessions. |\n498\t\n499\t```bash\n500\t# Start with defaults\n501\tagentscribe daemon start\n502\t\n503\t# Start with MCP server enabled\n504\tagentscribe daemon start --mcp\n505\t\n506\t# Start with debug logging\n507\tagentscribe daemon start --log-level debug\n508\t```\n509\t\n510\tOutput:\n511\t```\n512\tAgentScribe daemon started (PID 12345)\n513\t  Watching: 4 plugin source paths\n514\t  MCP: disabled\n515\t  Log: ~/.agentscribe/daemon.log\n516\t```\n517\t\n518\t#### `agentscribe daemon stop`\n519\t\n520\tStop the running daemon. Sends SIGTERM and waits for clean shutdown.\n521\t\n522\t| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n523\t|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n524\t| `--force` | | off | Send SIGKILL if the daemon doesn't stop within 5 seconds. |\n525\t\n526\t```bash\n527\tagentscribe daemon stop\n528\t```\n529\t\n530\tOutput:\n531\t```\n532\tStopping AgentScribe daemon (PID 12345)... stopped.\n533\t```\n534\t\n535\t#### `agentscribe daemon status`\n536\t\n537\tShow daemon state, resource usage, and activity.\n538\t\n539\t```bash\n540\tagentscribe daemon status\n541\t```\n542\t\n543\tOutput:\n544\t```\n545\tAgentScribe daemon (PID 12345)\n546\t  Status:     running\n547\t  Uptime:     3d 14h\n548\t  RSS:        12 MB\n549\t  Peak RSS:   47 MB\n550\t  MCP:        disabled\n551\t  Log:        ~/.agentscribe/daemon.log\n552\t\n553\t  Watches:    4 paths\n554\t  Last scrape: 2m ago (3 new sessions from claude-code)\n555\t  Total scrapes: 847 since start\n556\t  Errors:     0\n557\t```\n558\t\n559\tJSON (`--json`):\n560\t```json\n561\t{\n562\t  \"pid\": 12345,\n563\t  \"status\": \"running\",\n564\t  \"uptime_seconds\": 309600,\n565\t  \"rss_bytes\": 12582912,\n566\t  \"peak_rss_bytes\": 49283072,\n567\t  \"mcp_enabled\": false,\n568\t  \"log_path\": \"~/.agentscribe/daemon.log\",\n569\t  \"watches\": 4,\n570\t  \"last_scrape\": \"2026-03-16T12:28:00Z\",\n571\t  \"last_scrape_new_sessions\": 3,\n572\t  \"total_scrapes\": 847,\n573\t  \"errors\": 0\n574\t}\n575\t```\n576\t\n577\t#### `agentscribe daemon run`\n578\t\n579\tRun the daemon in the foreground. Use this when managing the process via systemd, supervisord, or similar. Does not daemonize, does not write a PID file. Logs to stderr.\n580\t\n581\t| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n582\t|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n583\t| `--mcp` | | off | Enable MCP server. |\n584\t| `--log-level <level>` | | `info` | Log level. |\n585\t| `--scrape-debounce <duration>` | | `5s` | Debounce period. |\n586\t\n587\t```bash\n588\t# Foreground (for systemd)\n589\tagentscribe daemon run\n590\t\n591\t# With MCP and debug logging\n592\tagentscribe daemon run --mcp --log-level debug\n593\t```\n594\t\n595\t#### `agentscribe daemon logs`\n596\t\n597\tTail the daemon log file. Convenience wrapper for reading `~/.agentscribe/daemon.log`.\n598\t\n599\t| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n600\t|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n601\t| `--follow` | `-f` | off | Follow new output (like `tail -f`). |\n602\t| `--lines <n>` | `-n` | `50` | Number of lines to show. |\n603\t| `--level <level>` | | all | Filter to this log level or above. |\n604\t\n605\t```bash\n606\t# Last 50 lines\n607\tagentscribe daemon logs\n608\t\n609\t# Follow in real time\n610\tagentscribe daemon logs -f\n611\t\n612\t# Only errors\n613\tagentscribe daemon logs --level error -n 100\n614\t```\n615\t\n616\t### Exit Codes\n617\t\n618\t| Code | Meaning |\n619\t|------|---------|\n620\t| 0 | Success |\n621\t| 1 | Daemon not running (for `stop`, `status`) or failed to start |\n622\t| 2 | PID file exists but process is dead (stale PID) — cleaned up automatically |\n623\t\n624\t---\n625\t\n626\t## `agentscribe plugins`\n627\t\n628\tManage scraper plugin definitions.\n629\t\n630\t### Usage\n631\t\n632\t```\n633\tagentscribe plugins <subcommand> [options]\n634\t```\n635\t\n636\t### Subcommands\n637\t\n638\t#### `agentscribe plugins list`\n639\t\n640\tShow all registered plugins, their source paths, and whether their paths match any files.\n641\t\n642\t```bash\n643\tagentscribe plugins list\n644\t```\n645\t\n646\tOutput:\n647\t```\n648\tPlugins (4 registered):\n649\t\n650\t  claude-code  v1.0  jsonl       ~/.claude/projects/*/*.jsonl           → 101 files matched\n651\t  aider        v1.0  markdown    ~/projects/*/.aider.chat.history.md    → 3 files matched\n652\t  codex        v1.0  jsonl       ~/.codex/sessions/**/*.jsonl           → 0 files matched\n653\t  opencode     v1.0  sqlite      ~/.local/share/opencode/storage/**     → 0 files matched\n654\t\n655\tPlugin dir: ~/.agentscribe/plugins/\n656\t```\n657\t\n658\tJSON (`--json`):\n659\t```json\n660\t{\n661\t  \"plugin_dir\": \"~/.agentscribe/plugins/\",\n662\t  \"plugins\": [\n663\t    {\n664\t      \"name\": \"claude-code\",\n665\t      \"version\": \"1.0\",\n666\t      \"format\": \"jsonl\",\n667\t      \"source_paths\": [\"~/.claude/projects/*/*.jsonl\"],\n668\t      \"matched_files\": 101,\n669\t      \"config_path\": \"~/.agentscribe/plugins/claude-code.toml\"\n670\t    }\n671\t  ]\n672\t}\n673\t```\n674\t\n675\t#### `agentscribe plugins validate <path>`\n676\t\n677\tValidate a plugin TOML file for correctness. Checks required fields, format compatibility, glob pattern resolution, field mapping syntax, and role map target values.\n678\t\n679\t| Argument | Required | Description |\n680\t|----------|----------|-------------|\n681\t| `<path>` | yes | Path to the plugin TOML file to validate. |\n682\t\n683\t```bash\n684\tagentscribe plugins validate ~/.agentscribe/plugins/pilot.toml\n685\t```\n686\t\n687\tOutput (success):\n688\t```\n689\tValidating pilot.toml...\n690\t  [ok] Required fields present\n691\t  [ok] Format \"jsonl\" is supported\n692\t  [ok] Source paths resolve to 14 files\n693\t  [ok] Session detection method \"one-file-per-session\" is valid\n694\t  [ok] Field mappings use valid dot-notation\n695\t  [ok] Role map targets are valid canonical roles\n696\t  [ok] No conflicting include/exclude type filters\n697\t\n698\tValid. Ready to scrape.\n699\t```\n700\t\n701\tOutput (errors):\n702\t```\n703\tValidating broken.toml...\n704\t  [ok] Required fields present\n705\t  [ok] Format \"jsonl\" is supported\n706\t  [WARN] Source paths resolve to 0 files — check that the paths exist\n707\t  [ERR] Field mapping \"role\" references \"msg.speaker\" but no \"msg\" object found in sample data\n708\t  [ERR] Role map target \"bot\" is not a valid canonical role (expected: user, assistant, system, tool_call, tool_result)\n709\t\n710\t2 errors, 1 warning. Fix errors before scraping.\n711\t```\n712\t\n713\t#### `agentscribe plugins show <name>`\n714\t\n715\tPrint the full plugin configuration.\n716\t\n717\t```bash\n718\tagentscribe plugins show claude-code\n719\t```\n720\t\n721\tOutput:\n722\t```\n723\tPlugin: claude-code (v1.0)\n724\tConfig: ~/.agentscribe/plugins/claude-code.toml\n725\t\n726\t[source]\n727\t  paths   = [\"~/.claude/projects/*/*.jsonl\"]\n728\t  exclude = [\"*/subagents/*\"]\n729\t  format  = jsonl\n730\t\n731\t[source.session_detection]\n732\t  method          = one-file-per-session\n733\t  session_id_from = filename\n734\t\n735\t[parser]\n736\t  timestamp = timestamp\n737\t  role      = message.role\n738\t  content   = message.content\n739\t  type      = type\n740\t\n741\t[parser.static]\n742\t  source_agent = claude-code\n743\t\n744\t[metadata]\n745\t  session_meta   = ~/.claude/usage-data/session-meta/{session_id}.json\n746\t  session_facets = ~/.claude/usage-data/facets/{session_id}.json\n747\t```\n748\t\n749\t### Exit Codes\n750\t\n751\t| Code | Meaning |\n752\t|------|---------|\n753\t| 0 | Success (or validation passed) |\n754\t| 1 | Validation failed with errors |\n755\t| 2 | Plugin file not found |\n756\t\n757\t---\n758\t\n759\t## `agentscribe config`\n760\t\n761\tView and modify global configuration.\n762\t\n763\t### Usage\n764\t\n765\t```\n766\tagentscribe config <subcommand> [options]\n767\t```\n768\t\n769\t### Subcommands\n770\t\n771\t#### `agentscribe config show`\n772\t\n773\tPrint the current global configuration.\n774\t\n775\t```bash\n776\tagentscribe config show\n777\t```\n778\t\n779\tOutput:\n780\t```\n781\tConfig: ~/.agentscribe/config.toml\n782\t\n783\t[general]\n784\t  data_dir = ~/.agentscribe\n785\t  log_level = info\n786\t\n787\t[scrape]\n788\t  debounce = 5s\n789\t  default_heap_size_mb = 50\n790\t\n791\t[index]\n792\t  tantivy_heap_size_mb = 50\n793\t\n794\t[daemon]\n795\t  mcp = false\n796\t  mcp_socket = ~/.agentscribe/mcp.sock\n797\t\n798\t[sqlite]\n799\t  cache_size_pages = 2000\n800\t```\n801\t\n802\t#### `agentscribe config set <key> <value>`\n803\t\n804\tSet a configuration value.\n805\t\n806\t| Argument | Required | Description |\n807\t|----------|----------|-------------|\n808\t| `<key>` | yes | Dot-notation config key (e.g., `daemon.mcp`, `index.tantivy_heap_size_mb`). |\n809\t| `<value>` | yes | Value to set. Type is inferred (boolean, integer, string). |\n810\t\n811\t```bash\n812\t# Enable MCP on daemon\n813\tagentscribe config set daemon.mcp true\n814\t\n815\t# Increase Tantivy writer heap\n816\tagentscribe config set index.tantivy_heap_size_mb 100\n817\t\n818\t# Change SQLite page cache\n819\tagentscribe config set sqlite.cache_size_pages 4000\n820\t```\n821\t\n822\tOutput:\n823\t```\n824\tSet daemon.mcp = true in ~/.agentscribe/config.toml\n825\t```\n826\t\n827\t#### `agentscribe config get <key>`\n828\t\n829\tGet a single configuration value.\n830\t\n831\t```bash\n832\tagentscribe config get daemon.mcp\n833\t```\n834\t\n835\tOutput:\n836\t```\n837\ttrue\n838\t```\n839\t\n840\t#### `agentscribe config init`\n841\t\n842\tCreate the data directory and default config file. Run once after installing AgentScribe. Copies bundled plugins to the plugins directory.\n843\t\n844\t```bash\n845\tagentscribe config init\n846\t```\n847\t\n848\tOutput:\n849\t```\n850\tCreated ~/.agentscribe/\n851\tCreated ~/.agentscribe/config.toml (default config)\n852\tCreated ~/.agentscribe/plugins/ (4 bundled plugins)\n853\t  claude-code.toml\n854\t  aider.toml\n855\t  opencode.toml\n856\t  codex.toml\n857\tCreated ~/.agentscribe/sessions/\n858\tCreated ~/.agentscribe/index/\n859\tCreated ~/.agentscribe/state/\n860\t\n861\tAgentScribe initialized. Run `agentscribe scrape` to start.\n862\t```\n863\t\n864\t| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n865\t|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n866\t| `--force` | | off | Overwrite existing config and plugins. Does not delete session data or the index. |\n867\t\n868\t### Exit Codes\n869\t\n870\t| Code | Meaning |\n871\t|------|---------|\n872\t| 0 | Success |\n873\t| 1 | Invalid key or value |\n874\t| 2 | Config file not found (for `show`, `get`, `set` — run `config init` first) |\n875\t\n876\t---\n877\t\n878\t## `agentscribe summarize`\n879\t\n880\tGenerate or regenerate a Markdown summary for a session. (Phase 3 feature.)\n881\t\n882\t### Usage\n883\t\n884\t```\n885\tagentscribe summarize <session-id> [options]\n886\t```\n887\t\n888\t### Arguments\n889\t\n890\t| Argument | Required | Description |\n891\t|----------|----------|-------------|\n892\t| `<session-id>` | yes | Session ID in `<agent>/<id>` format. |\n893\t\n894\t### Options\n895\t\n896\t| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n897\t|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n898\t| `--force` | `-f` | off | Regenerate even if a summary already exists. |\n899\t| `--method <method>` | | `extractive` | Summarization method: `extractive` (keyword/heuristic, no external deps) or `llm` (requires configured LLM endpoint). |\n900\t| `--stdout` | | off | Print summary to stdout instead of writing to the session's `.md` file. |\n901\t\n902\t### Examples\n903\t\n904\t```bash\n905\t# Summarize a session\n906\tagentscribe summarize claude-code/83f5a4e7\n907\t\n908\t# Regenerate with LLM-powered summarization\n909\tagentscribe summarize claude-code/83f5a4e7 --force --method llm\n910\t\n911\t# Preview without writing\n912\tagentscribe summarize claude-code/83f5a4e7 --stdout\n913\t```\n914\t\n915\tOutput:\n916\t```\n917\tSummary written to ~/.agentscribe/sessions/claude-code/83f5a4e7.md\n918\t```\n919\t\n920\t### Exit Codes\n921\t\n922\t| Code | Meaning |\n923\t|------|---------|\n924\t| 0 | Success |\n925\t| 1 | Session not found |\n926\t| 2 | Summary already exists (use `--force` to overwrite) |\n927\t\n928\t---\n929\t\n930\t## `agentscribe recurring`\n931\t\n932\tDetect recurring problems by grouping error fingerprints across sessions. Overridden by `AGENTSCRIBE_DATA_DIR` env var. |\n| `--config <path>` | `-c` | `~/.agentscribe/config.toml` | Path to global config file. |\n| `--json` | `-j` | off | Output in JSON format. Applies to all commands. When enabled, all output is machine-readable JSON — no human-formatted tables or progress bars. |\n| `--quiet` | `-q` | off | Suppress non-essential output. Errors still print to stderr. |\n| `--verbose` | `-v` | off | Enable debug-level logging to stderr. Repeatable (`-vv` for trace). |\n| `--color <when>` | | `auto` | Color output: `auto`, `always`, `never`. Auto-detects terminal. |\n| `--help` | `-h` | | Show help for the current command. |\n| `--version` | `-V` | | Print version and exit. |\n\n---\n\n## `agentscribe scrape`\n\nDiscover agent log files, parse them, normalize to canonical format, and write to the sessions directory. Updates the Tantivy index incrementally.\n\n### Usage\n\n```\nagentscribe scrape [options]\n```\n\n### Options\n\n| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n| `--plugin <name>` | `-p` | all plugins | Scrape only the named plugin. Can be repeated (`-p claude-code -p aider`). |\n| `--project <path>` | | all projects | Scrape only sessions from the given project directory. Matches against the session's `project` field. |\n| `--file <path>` | | | Scrape a single source file. Useful for testing a plugin against one log file. Requires `--plugin`. |\n| `--dry-run` | `-n` | off | Show what would be scraped without writing any files or updating the index. |\n| `--output-events` | | off | With `--dry-run`, print each parsed event as a JSON object to stdout. Use to verify field mapping. |\n| `--force` | `-f` | off | Ignore scrape state (last-seen offsets) and re-scrape everything. Does not delete existing sessions — deduplicates by session ID. |\n| `--no-index` | | off | Write session files but skip Tantivy index update. Useful for bulk imports where you'll `index rebuild` afterward. |\n| `--since <datetime>` | | | Only scrape sessions with activity after this timestamp. ISO 8601 or relative (`24h`, `7d`, `1w`). |\n\n### Examples\n\n```bash\n# Scrape all configured plugins\nagentscribe scrape\n\n# Scrape only Claude Code sessions\nagentscribe scrape --plugin claude-code\n\n# Dry-run with event output to verify a new plugin\nagentscribe scrape --plugin pilot --dry-run --output-events\n\n# Scrape a single file for debugging\nagentscribe scrape --plugin aider --file ~/myproject/.aider.chat.history.md\n\n# Re-scrape everything from scratch\nagentscribe scrape --force\n\n# Bulk import without indexing (rebuild index after)\nagentscribe scrape --force --no-index\nagentscribe index rebuild\n```\n\n### Output\n\nHuman-readable (default):\n```\nScraping claude-code...\n  Found 12 new sessions (skipped 89 unchanged)\n  Wrote 12 session files to ~/.agentscribe/sessions/claude-code/\nScraping aider...\n  Found 3 new sessions (skipped 5 unchanged)\n  Wrote 3 session files to ~/.agentscribe/sessions/aider/\nIndex updated: 15 documents added (1,262 total)\n```\n\nJSON (`--json`):\n```json\n{\n  \"plugins\": [\n    {\n      \"name\": \"claude-code\",\n      \"new_sessions\": 12,\n      \"skipped_sessions\": 89,\n      \"errors\": []\n    },\n    {\n      \"name\": \"aider\",\n      \"new_sessions\": 3,\n      \"skipped_sessions\": 5,\n      \"errors\": []\n    }\n  ],\n  \"index\": {\n    \"documents_added\": 15,\n    \"total_documents\": 1262\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Exit Codes\n\n| Code | Meaning |\n|------|---------|\n| 0 | Success — all plugins scraped without errors |\n| 1 | Partial failure — some plugins had errors, others succeeded. Check `errors` in JSON output. |\n| 2 | Total failure — no sessions scraped. Likely a config or permissions issue. |\n\n---\n\n## `agentscribe search`\n\nQuery the Tantivy index for matching sessions. The primary interface for agents seeking past solutions.\n\n### Usage\n\n```\nagentscribe search <query> [options]\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n| Argument | Required | Description |\n|----------|----------|-------------|\n| `<query>` | no* | Search query string. Supports Tantivy query syntax: `+required -excluded \"exact phrase\"`, field-scoped queries (`content:migration`), boolean operators (`AND`, `OR`, `NOT`), fuzzy terms (`migrat~1`), wildcard (`migrat*`). Required unless using `--error`, `--code`, `--solution-only`, `--like`, or `--session`. |\n\n### Options\n\n| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n| `--error <pattern>` | | | Search error fingerprints. Matches against normalized error patterns (e.g., `ConnectionError:Connection refused`). |\n| `--code <query>` | | | Search extracted code artifacts by content. |\n| `--lang <language>` | | | Language filter for `--code` search (e.g., `rust`, `python`, `typescript`). |\n| `--solution-only` | | off | Return only sessions that have an extracted solution. |\n| `--like <session-id>` | | | Find sessions similar to the given session ID using TF-IDF similarity. |\n| `--session <id>` | | | Retrieve a specific session by ID. Ignores query and filters. Returns the full session content. |\n| `--max-results <n>` | `-n` | `10` | Maximum number of sessions to return. |\n| `--snippet-length <n>` | | `200` | Maximum character length of content snippets per result. Set to `0` to omit snippets. |\n| `--token-budget <n>` | | | Token budget for greedy knapsack context packing. Optimally packs results within the token limit. |\n| `--agent <name>` | `-a` | all | Filter to sessions from this agent type. Can be repeated. |\n| `--project <path>` | | all | Filter to sessions from this project directory. |\n| `--since <datetime>` | | | Only match sessions after this timestamp. ISO 8601 or relative (`24h`, `7d`, `1w`). |\n| `--before <datetime>` | | | Only match sessions before this timestamp. |\n| `--tag <tag>` | `-t` | | Filter by tag. Can be repeated (AND logic). |\n| `--outcome <outcome>` | | | Filter by session outcome: `success`, `failure`, `abandoned`, `unknown`. |\n| `--type <type>` | | all | Filter by document type: `session`, `code_artifact`. |\n| `--model <name>` | | all | Filter by LLM model name. |\n| `--sort <field>` | `-s` | `relevance` | Sort order: `relevance` (BM25 score), `newest`, `oldest`, `turns`. |\n| `--offset <n>` | | `0` | Skip first N results. For pagination. |\n| `--fuzzy` | | off | Enable fuzzy matching on all query terms (Levenshtein distance 1). Useful when agents don't know exact terminology. |\n\n### Examples\n\n```bash\n# Basic search\nagentscribe search \"postgres migration\"\n\n# Agent-oriented: JSON output, limited results, short snippets\nagentscribe search \"database connection timeout\" --json -n 3 --snippet-length 150\n\n# Scoped to a specific agent and project\nagentscribe search \"deploy\" --agent claude-code --project /home/coding/myapp\n\n# Recent sessions only\nagentscribe search \"build failure\" --since 7d\n\n# Fuzzy search for misspellings or approximate terms\nagentscribe search \"kuberntes\" --fuzzy\n\n# Exact phrase search\nagentscribe search '\"connection pool exhausted\"'\n\n# Advanced Tantivy query syntax\nagentscribe search '+content:migration +agent:claude-code -content:rollback'\n\n# Retrieve a specific session's full content\nagentscribe search --session claude-code/83f5a4e7\n\n# Search by error fingerprint\nagentscribe search --error \"ConnectionError\"\n\n# Search code artifacts\nagentscribe search --code \"fn migrate\" --lang rust\n\n# Find sessions with extracted solutions\nagentscribe search \"auth token\" --solution-only\n\n# Find similar sessions\nagentscribe search --like claude-code/83f5a4e7\n\n# Context packing for agent prompts (fit within token budget)\nagentscribe search \"error handling\" --token-budget 4000 --json\n\n# Filter by document type and model\nagentscribe search \"refactor\" --type code_artifact --model claude-sonnet-4-20250514\n```\n\n### Output\n\nHuman-readable (default):\n```\n3 results for \"postgres migration\" (searched 1,262 sessions in 4ms)\n\n[1] claude-code/83f5a4e7  (score: 8.42)\n    Project:  /home/coding/myapp\n    Date:     2026-03-14 10:30\n    Turns:    42\n    Outcome:  success\n    Summary:  Migrated Postgres schema from v3 to v4, added rollback script\n    Snippet:  ...ran ALTER TABLE to add the new columns, then backfilled\n              existing rows. The migration took 3 minutes on a 2M row table...\n\n[2] aider/session-2026-03-10  (score: 6.18)\n    Project:  /home/coding/api-server\n    Date:     2026-03-10 14:15\n    Turns:    18\n    Outcome:  success\n    Summary:  Fixed Postgres connection pooling, added retry logic\n    Snippet:  ...the connection pool was exhausting under load because\n              max_connections was set to 10. Bumped to 50 and added...\n\n[3] codex/abc-thread-123  (score: 4.01)\n    Project:  /home/coding/data-pipeline\n    Date:     2026-03-08 09:00\n    Turns:    7\n    Outcome:  failure\n    Summary:  Attempted Postgres 14->16 upgrade, hit extension incompatibility\n    Snippet:  ...pg_trgm extension not available in pg16 container image.\n              Rolled back to pg14 and opened an issue...\n```\n\nJSON (`--json`):\n```json\n{\n  \"query\": \"postgres migration\",\n  \"total_matches\": 3,\n  \"search_time_ms\": 4,\n  \"sessions_searched\": 1262,\n  \"results\": [\n    {\n      \"session_id\": \"claude-code/83f5a4e7\",\n      \"source_agent\": \"claude-code\",\n      \"project\": \"/home/coding/myapp\",\n      \"timestamp\": \"2026-03-14T10:30:00Z\",\n      \"turns\": 42,\n      \"outcome\": \"success\",\n      \"score\": 8.42,\n      \"summary\": \"Migrated Postgres schema from v3 to v4, added rollback script\",\n      \"snippet\": \"...ran ALTER TABLE to add the new columns, then backfilled existing rows. The migration took 3 minutes on a 2M row table...\",\n      \"tags\": [\"postgres\", \"migration\", \"schema\", \"alter-table\"]\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n### Full Session Retrieval\n\nWhen `--session <id>` is used, returns the complete normalized conversation:\n\n```bash\nagentscribe search --session claude-code/83f5a4e7 --json\n```\n\n```json\n{\n  \"session_id\": \"claude-code/83f5a4e7\",\n  \"source_agent\": \"claude-code\",\n  \"project\": \"/home/coding/myapp\",\n  \"started\": \"2026-03-14T10:30:00Z\",\n  \"ended\": \"2026-03-14T11:15:00Z\",\n  \"turns\": 42,\n  \"outcome\": \"success\",\n  \"summary\": \"Migrated Postgres schema from v3 to v4, added rollback script\",\n  \"events\": [\n    {\n      \"ts\": \"2026-03-14T10:30:00Z\",\n      \"role\": \"user\",\n      \"content\": \"I need to migrate the Postgres schema from v3 to v4...\"\n    },\n    {\n      \"ts\": \"2026-03-14T10:30:15Z\",\n      \"role\": \"assistant\",\n      \"content\": \"I'll create a migration script that...\"\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n### Exit Codes\n\n| Code | Meaning |\n|------|---------|\n| 0 | Results found |\n| 0 | No results (empty results array, not an error) |\n| 1 | Query parse error or invalid filter |\n| 2 | Index not found — run `agentscribe scrape` first |\n\n---\n\n## `agentscribe index`\n\nManage the Tantivy search index.\n\n### Usage\n\n```\nagentscribe index <subcommand> [options]\n```\n\n### Subcommands\n\n#### `agentscribe index rebuild`\n\nDrop the existing Tantivy index and rebuild it from all normalized session files. Use after a bulk import, after changing the schema, or to recover from index corruption.\n\n| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n| `--plugin <name>` | `-p` | all | Only re-index sessions from this plugin. |\n| `--heap-size <mb>` | | `50` | Tantivy writer heap size in MB. Higher = faster indexing, more RAM. |\n\n```bash\n# Full rebuild\nagentscribe index rebuild\n\n# Rebuild only Claude Code sessions\nagentscribe index rebuild --plugin claude-code\n\n# Fast rebuild with more memory\nagentscribe index rebuild --heap-size 100\n```\n\nOutput:\n```\nDropping existing index...\nRebuilding from 1,262 session files...\n  [========================================] 1262/1262 (47/s)\nIndex rebuilt in 26.8s\n```\n\n#### `agentscribe index stats`\n\nShow index statistics.\n\n```bash\nagentscribe index stats\n```\n\nOutput:\n```\nTantivy index at ~/.agentscribe/index/tantivy/\n  Documents:    1,262\n  Segments:     4\n  Size on disk: 38 MB\n  Last updated: 2026-03-16 12:30:00\n  Fields:       content, summary, session_id, source_agent, project, tags, timestamp, turn_count, outcome\n```\n\nJSON (`--json`):\n```json\n{\n  \"path\": \"~/.agentscribe/index/tantivy/\",\n  \"documents\": 1262,\n  \"segments\": 4,\n  \"size_bytes\": 39845888,\n  \"last_updated\": \"2026-03-16T12:30:00Z\",\n  \"fields\": [\"content\", \"summary\", \"session_id\", \"source_agent\", \"project\", \"tags\", \"timestamp\", \"turn_count\", \"outcome\"]\n}\n```\n\n#### `agentscribe index optimize`\n\nForce-merge Tantivy segments for better query performance. Normally unnecessary — Tantivy auto-merges in the background.\n\n```bash\nagentscribe index optimize\n```\n\nOutput:\n```\nMerging 4 segments into 1... done (3.2s)\nIndex size: 38 MB -> 35 MB\n```\n\n### Exit Codes\n\n| Code | Meaning |\n|------|---------|\n| 0 | Success |\n| 1 | Index error (corruption, missing session files) |\n| 2 | No session files found — run `agentscribe scrape` first |\n\n---\n\n## `agentscribe status`\n\nShow a summary of what AgentScribe knows: tracked agents, session counts, last scrape time, daemon state, and disk usage.\n\n### Usage\n\n```\nagentscribe status [options]\n```\n\n### Options\n\n| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n| `--plugin <name>` | `-p` | all | Show status for a specific plugin only. |\n\n### Examples\n\n```bash\nagentscribe status\n```\n\nOutput:\n```\nAgentScribe v0.1.0\nData dir: ~/.agentscribe (142 MB)\n\nDaemon: running (PID 12345, uptime 3d 14h, RSS 12 MB)\n\nPlugins:\n  claude-code    89 sessions   last scraped 2m ago     ~/.claude/projects/*/*.jsonl\n  aider           8 sessions   last scraped 2m ago     ~/projects/*/.aider.chat.history.md\n  codex          14 sessions   last scraped 2m ago     ~/.codex/sessions/**/*.jsonl\n  opencode        0 sessions   never scraped           ~/.local/share/opencode/storage/\n\nIndex: 111 documents, 4 segments, 38 MB on disk\n\nScrape state: incremental (tracking offsets for 6 source paths)\n```\n\nJSON (`--json`):\n```json\n{\n  \"version\": \"0.1.0\",\n  \"data_dir\": \"~/.agentscribe\",\n  \"data_dir_bytes\": 148897792,\n  \"daemon\": {\n    \"running\": true,\n    \"pid\": 12345,\n    \"uptime_seconds\": 309600,\n    \"rss_bytes\": 12582912\n  },\n  \"plugins\": [\n    {\n      \"name\": \"claude-code\",\n      \"sessions\": 89,\n      \"last_scraped\": \"2026-03-16T12:28:00Z\",\n      \"source_paths\": [\"~/.claude/projects/*/*.jsonl\"]\n    }\n  ],\n  \"index\": {\n    \"documents\": 111,\n    \"segments\": 4,\n    \"size_bytes\": 39845888\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Exit Codes\n\n| Code | Meaning |\n|------|---------|\n| 0 | Success |\n| 1 | Data dir not found or not initialized |\n\n---\n\n## `agentscribe daemon`\n\nManage the background daemon that watches for new log data and scrapes automatically.\n\n### Usage\n\n```\nagentscribe daemon <subcommand> [options]\n```\n\n### Subcommands\n\n#### `agentscribe daemon start`\n\nStart the daemon in the background. Writes PID to `~/.agentscribe/agentscribe.pid`. Logs to `~/.agentscribe/daemon.log`.\n\n| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n| `--mcp` | | off | Enable MCP server on the daemon. Listens on a Unix socket at `~/.agentscribe/mcp.sock`. |\n| `--log-level <level>` | | `info` | Daemon log level: `error`, `warn`, `info`, `debug`, `trace`. |\n| `--scrape-debounce <duration>` | | `5s` | Wait this long after a file change before scraping. Prevents thrashing during active agent sessions. |\n\n```bash\n# Start with defaults\nagentscribe daemon start\n\n# Start with MCP server enabled\nagentscribe daemon start --mcp\n\n# Start with debug logging\nagentscribe daemon start --log-level debug\n```\n\nOutput:\n```\nAgentScribe daemon started (PID 12345)\n  Watching: 4 plugin source paths\n  MCP: disabled\n  Log: ~/.agentscribe/daemon.log\n```\n\n#### `agentscribe daemon stop`\n\nStop the running daemon. Sends SIGTERM and waits for clean shutdown.\n\n| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n| `--force` | | off | Send SIGKILL if the daemon doesn't stop within 5 seconds. |\n\n```bash\nagentscribe daemon stop\n```\n\nOutput:\n```\nStopping AgentScribe daemon (PID 12345)... stopped.\n```\n\n#### `agentscribe daemon status`\n\nShow daemon state, resource usage, and activity.\n\n```bash\nagentscribe daemon status\n```\n\nOutput:\n```\nAgentScribe daemon (PID 12345)\n  Status:     running\n  Uptime:     3d 14h\n  RSS:        12 MB\n  Peak RSS:   47 MB\n  MCP:        disabled\n  Log:        ~/.agentscribe/daemon.log\n\n  Watches:    4 paths\n  Last scrape: 2m ago (3 new sessions from claude-code)\n  Total scrapes: 847 since start\n  Errors:     0\n```\n\nJSON (`--json`):\n```json\n{\n  \"pid\": 12345,\n  \"status\": \"running\",\n  \"uptime_seconds\": 309600,\n  \"rss_bytes\": 12582912,\n  \"peak_rss_bytes\": 49283072,\n  \"mcp_enabled\": false,\n  \"log_path\": \"~/.agentscribe/daemon.log\",\n  \"watches\": 4,\n  \"last_scrape\": \"2026-03-16T12:28:00Z\",\n  \"last_scrape_new_sessions\": 3,\n  \"total_scrapes\": 847,\n  \"errors\": 0\n}\n```\n\n#### `agentscribe daemon run`\n\nRun the daemon in the foreground. Use this when managing the process via systemd, supervisord, or similar. Does not daemonize, does not write a PID file. Logs to stderr.\n\n| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n| `--mcp` | | off | Enable MCP server. |\n| `--log-level <level>` | | `info` | Log level. |\n| `--scrape-debounce <duration>` | | `5s` | Debounce period. |\n\n```bash\n# Foreground (for systemd)\nagentscribe daemon run\n\n# With MCP and debug logging\nagentscribe daemon run --mcp --log-level debug\n```\n\n#### `agentscribe daemon logs`\n\nTail the daemon log file. Convenience wrapper for reading `~/.agentscribe/daemon.log`.\n\n| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n| `--follow` | `-f` | off | Follow new output (like `tail -f`). |\n| `--lines <n>` | `-n` | `50` | Number of lines to show. |\n| `--level <level>` | | all | Filter to this log level or above. |\n\n```bash\n# Last 50 lines\nagentscribe daemon logs\n\n# Follow in real time\nagentscribe daemon logs -f\n\n# Only errors\nagentscribe daemon logs --level error -n 100\n```\n\n### Exit Codes\n\n| Code | Meaning |\n|------|---------|\n| 0 | Success |\n| 1 | Daemon not running (for `stop`, `status`) or failed to start |\n| 2 | PID file exists but process is dead (stale PID) — cleaned up automatically |\n\n---\n\n## `agentscribe plugins`\n\nManage scraper plugin definitions.\n\n### Usage\n\n```\nagentscribe plugins <subcommand> [options]\n```\n\n### Subcommands\n\n#### `agentscribe plugins list`\n\nShow all registered plugins, their source paths, and whether their paths match any files.\n\n```bash\nagentscribe plugins list\n```\n\nOutput:\n```\nPlugins (4 registered):\n\n  claude-code  v1.0  jsonl       ~/.claude/projects/*/*.jsonl           → 101 files matched\n  aider        v1.0  markdown    ~/projects/*/.aider.chat.history.md    → 3 files matched\n  codex        v1.0  jsonl       ~/.codex/sessions/**/*.jsonl           → 0 files matched\n  opencode     v1.0  sqlite      ~/.local/share/opencode/storage/**     → 0 files matched\n\nPlugin dir: ~/.agentscribe/plugins/\n```\n\nJSON (`--json`):\n```json\n{\n  \"plugin_dir\": \"~/.agentscribe/plugins/\",\n  \"plugins\": [\n    {\n      \"name\": \"claude-code\",\n      \"version\": \"1.0\",\n      \"format\": \"jsonl\",\n      \"source_paths\": [\"~/.claude/projects/*/*.jsonl\"],\n      \"matched_files\": 101,\n      \"config_path\": \"~/.agentscribe/plugins/claude-code.toml\"\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n#### `agentscribe plugins validate <path>`\n\nValidate a plugin TOML file for correctness. Checks required fields, format compatibility, glob pattern resolution, field mapping syntax, and role map target values.\n\n| Argument | Required | Description |\n|----------|----------|-------------|\n| `<path>` | yes | Path to the plugin TOML file to validate. |\n\n```bash\nagentscribe plugins validate ~/.agentscribe/plugins/pilot.toml\n```\n\nOutput (success):\n```\nValidating pilot.toml...\n  [ok] Required fields present\n  [ok] Format \"jsonl\" is supported\n  [ok] Source paths resolve to 14 files\n  [ok] Session detection method \"one-file-per-session\" is valid\n  [ok] Field mappings use valid dot-notation\n  [ok] Role map targets are valid canonical roles\n  [ok] No conflicting include/exclude type filters\n\nValid. Ready to scrape.\n```\n\nOutput (errors):\n```\nValidating broken.toml...\n  [ok] Required fields present\n  [ok] Format \"jsonl\" is supported\n  [WARN] Source paths resolve to 0 files — check that the paths exist\n  [ERR] Field mapping \"role\" references \"msg.speaker\" but no \"msg\" object found in sample data\n  [ERR] Role map target \"bot\" is not a valid canonical role (expected: user, assistant, system, tool_call, tool_result)\n\n2 errors, 1 warning. Fix errors before scraping.\n```\n\n#### `agentscribe plugins show <name>`\n\nPrint the full plugin configuration.\n\n```bash\nagentscribe plugins show claude-code\n```\n\nOutput:\n```\nPlugin: claude-code (v1.0)\nConfig: ~/.agentscribe/plugins/claude-code.toml\n\n[source]\n  paths   = [\"~/.claude/projects/*/*.jsonl\"]\n  exclude = [\"*/subagents/*\"]\n  format  = jsonl\n\n[source.session_detection]\n  method          = one-file-per-session\n  session_id_from = filename\n\n[parser]\n  timestamp = timestamp\n  role      = message.role\n  content   = message.content\n  type      = type\n\n[parser.static]\n  source_agent = claude-code\n\n[metadata]\n  session_meta   = ~/.claude/usage-data/session-meta/{session_id}.json\n  session_facets = ~/.claude/usage-data/facets/{session_id}.json\n```\n\n### Exit Codes\n\n| Code | Meaning |\n|------|---------|\n| 0 | Success (or validation passed) |\n| 1 | Validation failed with errors |\n| 2 | Plugin file not found |\n\n---\n\n## `agentscribe config`\n\nView and modify global configuration.\n\n### Usage\n\n```\nagentscribe config <subcommand> [options]\n```\n\n### Subcommands\n\n#### `agentscribe config show`\n\nPrint the current global configuration.\n\n```bash\nagentscribe config show\n```\n\nOutput:\n```\nConfig: ~/.agentscribe/config.toml\n\n[general]\n  data_dir = ~/.agentscribe\n  log_level = info\n\n[scrape]\n  debounce = 5s\n  default_heap_size_mb = 50\n\n[index]\n  tantivy_heap_size_mb = 50\n\n[daemon]\n  mcp = false\n  mcp_socket = ~/.agentscribe/mcp.sock\n\n[sqlite]\n  cache_size_pages = 2000\n```\n\n#### `agentscribe config set <key> <value>`\n\nSet a configuration value.\n\n| Argument | Required | Description |\n|----------|----------|-------------|\n| `<key>` | yes | Dot-notation config key (e.g., `daemon.mcp`, `index.tantivy_heap_size_mb`). |\n| `<value>` | yes | Value to set. Type is inferred (boolean, integer, string). |\n\n```bash\n# Enable MCP on daemon\nagentscribe config set daemon.mcp true\n\n# Increase Tantivy writer heap\nagentscribe config set index.tantivy_heap_size_mb 100\n\n# Change SQLite page cache\nagentscribe config set sqlite.cache_size_pages 4000\n```\n\nOutput:\n```\nSet daemon.mcp = true in ~/.agentscribe/config.toml\n```\n\n#### `agentscribe config get <key>`\n\nGet a single configuration value.\n\n```bash\nagentscribe config get daemon.mcp\n```\n\nOutput:\n```\ntrue\n```\n\n#### `agentscribe config init`\n\nCreate the data directory and default config file. Run once after installing AgentScribe. Copies bundled plugins to the plugins directory.\n\n```bash\nagentscribe config init\n```\n\nOutput:\n```\nCreated ~/.agentscribe/\nCreated ~/.agentscribe/config.toml (default config)\nCreated ~/.agentscribe/plugins/ (4 bundled plugins)\n  claude-code.toml\n  aider.toml\n  opencode.toml\n  codex.toml\nCreated ~/.agentscribe/sessions/\nCreated ~/.agentscribe/index/\nCreated ~/.agentscribe/state/\n\nAgentScribe initialized. Run `agentscribe scrape` to start.\n```\n\n| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n| `--force` | | off | Overwrite existing config and plugins. Does not delete session data or the index. |\n\n### Exit Codes\n\n| Code | Meaning |\n|------|---------|\n| 0 | Success |\n| 1 | Invalid key or value |\n| 2 | Config file not found (for `show`, `get`, `set` — run `config init` first) |\n\n---\n\n## `agentscribe summarize`\n\nGenerate or regenerate a Markdown summary for a session. (Phase 3 feature.)\n\n### Usage\n\n```\nagentscribe summarize <session-id> [options]\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n| Argument | Required | Description |\n|----------|----------|-------------|\n| `<session-id>` | yes | Session ID in `<agent>/<id>` format. |\n\n### Options\n\n| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n| `--force` | `-f` | off | Regenerate even if a summary already exists. |\n| `--method <method>` | | `extractive` | Summarization method: `extractive` (keyword/heuristic, no external deps) or `llm` (requires configured LLM endpoint). |\n| `--stdout` | | off | Print summary to stdout instead of writing to the session's `.md` file. |\n\n### Examples\n\n```bash\n# Summarize a session\nagentscribe summarize claude-code/83f5a4e7\n\n# Regenerate with LLM-powered summarization\nagentscribe summarize claude-code/83f5a4e7 --force --method llm\n\n# Preview without writing\nagentscribe summarize claude-code/83f5a4e7 --stdout\n```\n\nOutput:\n```\nSummary written to ~/.agentscribe/sessions/claude-code/83f5a4e7.md\n```\n\n### Exit Codes\n\n| Code | Meaning |\n|------|---------|\n| 0 | Success |\n| 1 | Session not found |\n| 2 | Summary already exists (use `--force` to overwrite) |\n\n---\n\n## `agentscribe recurring`\n\nDetect recurring problems by grouping error fingerprints across sessions. Shows problems that happen repeatedly, which projects they affect, and links to sessions that fixed them.\n\n### Usage\n\n```\nagentscribe recurring [options]\n```\n\n### Options\n\n| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n| `--since <datetime>` | | `30d` | Only consider sessions after this timestamp. ISO 8601 or relative (`30d`, `12w`). |\n| `--threshold <n>` | | `3` | Minimum occurrence count to report. Problems with fewer occurrences are excluded. |\n| `--json` | | off | Output in JSON format. |\n\n### Examples\n\n```bash\n# Find recurring problems in the last 30 days\nagentscribe recurring\n\n# Only problems that occurred 5+ times\nagentscribe recurring --threshold 5\n\n# Last 90 days\nagentscribe recurring --since 90d\n\n# JSON for scripting\nagentscribe recurring --since 30d --json\n```\n\n### Output\n\nHuman-readable (default):\n```\nRecurring Problems (since 2026-02-20, threshold: 3)\n\n[1] ConnectionError:Connection refused to {host}:{port}\n    Occurrences: 5 sessions, 12 events\n    Projects:    myapp, api-server\n    Agents:      claude-code, aider\n    Fixed by:    claude-code\n    Last seen:   2026-03-15\n    Last fix:    claude-code/abc123 (2026-03-15)\n\n[2] TypeError:Cannot read properties of undefined (reading 'map')\n    Occurrences: 3 sessions, 7 events\n    Projects:    frontend\n    Agents:      claude-code\n    Fixed by:    (none)\n    Last seen:   2026-03-12\n```\n\nJSON (`--json`):\n```json\n{\n  \"since\": \"2026-02-20T00:00:00Z\",\n  \"threshold\": 3,\n  \"problems\": [\n    {\n      \"fingerprint\": \"ConnectionError:Connection refused to {host}:{port}\",\n      \"session_count\": 5,\n      \"event_count\": 12,\n      \"projects\": [\"myapp\", \"api-server\"],\n      \"agents\": [\"claude-code\", \"aider\"],\n      \"fix_agents\": [\"claude-code\"],\n      \"last_seen\": \"2026-03-15T10:30:00Z\",\n      \"last_fix_session\": \"claude-code/abc123\",\n      \"last_fix_at\": \"2026-03-15T10:45:00Z\"\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n### Exit Codes\n\n| Code | Meaning |\n|------|---------|\n| 0 | Success |\n| 0 | No recurring problems found (empty array) |\n| 1 | Data dir not initialized |\n| 2 | No sessions found in the time range |\n\n---\n\n## `agentscribe rules`\n\nDistill patterns from past agent sessions into project-specific rules files. Analyzes past sessions to extract corrections, conventions, context hints, and warnings.\n\n### Usage\n\n```\nagentscribe rules <project-path> [options]\n```\n\n### Arguments\n\n| Argument | Required | Description |\n|----------|----------|-------------|\n| `<project-path>` | yes | Path to the project directory to extract rules for. |\n\n### Options\n\n| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n| `--format <format>` | | `claude` | Output format: `claude` (CLAUDE.md), `cursor` (.cursorrules), or `aider` (.aider.conf.yml). |\n| `--json` | | off | Output rules as JSON without writing to a file. |\n\n### Examples\n\n```bash\n# Generate CLAUDE.md rules for a project\nagentscribe rules ~/my-project --format claude\n\n# Generate .cursorrules\nagentscribe rules ~/my-project --format cursor\n\n# Preview rules without writing\nagentscribe rules ~/my-project --json\n```\n\n### Output\n\nHuman-readable (default):\n```\nWrote 12 rules to ~/my-project/CLAUDE.md (47 sessions analyzed)\n```\n\nJSON (`--json`):\n```json\n{\n  \"project_path\": \"/home/user/my-project\",\n  \"sessions_analyzed\": 47,\n  \"rules\": [\n    {\"type\": \"correction\", \"rule\": \"Use `uuid v7` for all new ID columns, not v4\"},\n    {\"type\": \"convention\", \"rule\": \"API endpoints use kebab-case URLs, snake_case response fields\"},\n    {\"type\": \"context\", \"rule\": \"The `legacy` module wraps the old PHP API — don't refactor it\"},\n    {\"type\": \"warning\", \"rule\": \"Don't modify migration files after they've been applied\"}\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n### Exit Codes\n\n| Code | Meaning |\n|------|---------|\n| 0 | Success (rules written or output) |\n| 1 | No sessions found for the project |\n| 2 | Data dir not initialized |\n\n---\n\n## `agentscribe analytics`\n\nCross-agent performance comparison and analytics. Reports success rates, specialization patterns, cost estimates, and weekly trends.\n\n### Usage\n\n```\nagentscribe analytics [options]\n```\n\n### Options\n\n| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n| `--agent <name>` | `-a` | all | Filter to a specific agent. |\n| `--project <path>` | `-p` | all | Filter to sessions from this project directory. |\n| `--since <datetime>` | | all time | Only include sessions after this date. ISO 8601 or relative (`30d`, `12w`). |\n| `--json` | | off | Output in JSON format. |\n\n### Examples\n\n```bash\n# Overall analytics\nagentscribe analytics\n\n# Specific agent\nagentscribe analytics --agent claude-code\n\n# Last 30 days\nagentscribe analytics --since 30d\n\n# Specific project\nagentscribe analytics --project ~/my-project\n\n# JSON for dashboards\nagentscribe analytics --since 30d --json\n```\n\n### Output\n\nHuman-readable (default):\n```\nAgentScribe Analytics (2026-02-20 to 2026-03-20)\n\nTotal sessions: 47 | Success rate: 80.9% | Avg turns: 12.3\n\nAgent Breakdown:\n  claude-code    31 sessions  83.9% success  10.5 avg turns (success)  ~$2.50 est. cost\n  aider           8 sessions  75.0% success  14.2 avg turns (success)  ~$0.80 est. cost\n  codex           8 digest`\n\nGenerate an activity digest summary over a configurable time period. Produces a Markdown report suitable for a 2-minute skim.\n\n### Usage\n\n```\nagentscribe digest [options]\n```\n\n### Options\n\n| Option | Short | Default | Description |\n|--------|-------|---------|-------------|\n| `--since <period>` | | `7d` | Time period to cover. ISO 8601 or relative (`7d`, `30d`, `12w`). |\n| `--output <path>` | `-o` | stdout | Write output to a file instead of printing to stdout. |\n| `--json` | | off | Output in JSON format instead of Markdown. |\n\n### Examples\n\n```bash\n# Weekly digest to stdout\nagentscribe digest --since 7d\n\n# Save monthly digest to file\nagentscribe digest --since 30d --output ~/reports/march-digest.md\n\n# JSON for custom processing\nagentscribe digest --since 7d --json\n```\n\n### Output\n\nThe Markdown digest includes:\n- Session counts by agent and project\n- Recurring problems detected\n- Agent comparison table\n- Most-touched files\n- New error patterns discovered\n- Token usage and estimated costs\n\n### Exit Codes\n\n| Code | Meaning |\n|------|---------|\n| 0 | Success |\n| 1 | Data dir not initialized |\n| 2 | No sessions in the time range |\n\n---\n\n## Environment Variables\n\n| Variable | Description |\n|----------|-------------|\n| `AGENTSCRIBE_DATA_DIR` | Override the data directory (default: `~/.agentscribe`). Takes precedence over `--data-dir` flag. |\n| `AGENTSCRIBE_LOG` | Set log level for CLI commands: `error`, `warn`, `info`, `debug`, `trace`. token count for a string section.\n    pub fn count_tokens(text: &str) -> usize {\n        text.chars().count().div_ceil(CHARS_PER_TOKEN)\n    }\n\n    /// Create a budget-aware version of the pack with priority ordering.\n    pub fn with_budget(mut self, budget: usize) -> Self {\n        let solution_tokens = Self::count_tokens(&self.past_solutions);\n        let conventions_tokens = Self::count_tokens(&self.conventions);\n        let file_notes_tokens = Self::count_tokens(&self.file_notes);\n\n        // Priority: past solutions > conventions > file notes\n        let mut remaining = budget;\n\n        // Always include past solutions (highest priority)\n        if solution_tokens > remaining {\n            // Truncate solutions to fit budget\n            let max_chars = remaining * CHARS_PER_TOKEN;\n            self.past_solutions = truncate_to_chars(&self.past_solutions, max_chars);\n            remaining = 0;\n        } else {\n            remaining -= solution_tokens;\n        }\n\n        // Include conventions if budget remains\n        if remaining > 0 && !self.conventions.is_empty() {\n            if conventions_tokens > remaining {\n                let max_chars = remaining * CHARS_PER_TOKEN;\n                self.conventions = truncate_to_chars(&self.conventions, max_chars);\n                remaining = 0;\n            } else {\n
